    <script type="text/javascript">
     function isConsentGiven() {
		if ('consentIsGiven' in window && (consentIsGiven === true || consentIsGiven === false))
			return consentIsGiven;
		if (!('_iub' in window && 'csConfiguration' in _iub))
			return false;
		var siteId = _iub.csConfiguration.siteId || '';
		var cookiePolicyId = _iub.csConfiguration.cookiePolicyId || '';
		var cs = document.cookie.split(';');
		var consentIsGiven = false;
		for (var i = 0; i < cs.length; i++) {
			while (cs[i].charAt(0) == ' ')
			cs[i] = cs[i].substring(1);
			if (cs[i].indexOf('_iub_cs-s' + siteId) == 0 || cs[i].indexOf('_iub_cs-' + cookiePolicyId) == 0) {
				consentIsGiven = true;
				break;
			}
		}
		window.consentIsGiven = consentIsGiven;
		return consentIsGiven;
	}

	//alert(isConsentGiven());
    </script>

		var noADV = false;

min = dd.getMinutes();
hour = dd.getHours(); 
curr_min = min < 10 ? "0"+min : min;
curr_hour = hour < 10 ? "0"+hour : hour;

function itDate() 
{
	 // 21 Settembre 2009, 12:28
	//data = dd.getDate() + " " + mm[(dd.getMonth())] + " " + dd.getFullYear() + ", " + dd.getHours() + ":" + dd.getMinutes();
	data = "<em class='date'>" + 
		gg[(dd.getDay())] + 
		", " + 
		dd.getDate() + 
		" " + mm[(dd.getMonth())] + " " + 
		dd.getFullYear() + 
		"</em><strong class='time'>" + curr_hour + ":" + curr_min + "</strong>";
	return data
       //$('#itdate').html(data);
}
document.write(itDate());

      <div id="menuMobile">

      <script type="text/javascript">
       if (navigator.userAgent.indexOf('Android 3.') == -1 || navigator.userAgent.indexOf('iPhone') != -1 || navigator.userAgent.indexOf('Ansa ClickToNews') != -1) {
		$('.btn-hamburger').attr('style', 'display:none!important');
		//$('.bot-menu').attr('style', 'display:none!important');
		$('.cd-search').attr('style', 'display:block!important');
		$('.header-mobile').detach().insertBefore($('#4w-skin-header'));
		$('#menuMobile').append('<script src=\'/sito/js/menu_top/util.js\'><\/script>');
		$('#menuMobile').append('<script src=\'/sito/js/menu_top/menu-aim.js\'><\/script>');
		$('#menuMobile').append('<script src=\'/sito/js/menu_top/main.js\'><\/script>');
		
	} else {
		$('.menu-top-mobile').attr('style', 'display:none!important');
		$('.header').attr('style', 'display:block!important');
		$('.bot-menu').attr('style', 'display:block!important');
		$('.header-mobile').attr('style', 'display:none!important');
		$('.inner-section').attr('style', 'padding-top:0');
		$('.cd-nav-trigger').attr('style', 'display:none!important');
		$('.cd-search').attr('style', 'display:none!important');		
	}
	
	var c, currentScrollTop = 0, navbar = $('.menu-top-mobile');

	$(window).scroll(function() {
		var a = $(window).scrollTop();
		var b = navbar.height();

		currentScrollTop = a;

		if (currentScrollTop == 0) {
			navbar.removeClass("scrollUp");
		} else if (c < currentScrollTop && a > b + b || currentScrollTop == 0) {
			navbar.removeClass("scrollUp").addClass("scrollDown");
		} else if (c > currentScrollTop && !(a <= b)) {
			navbar.removeClass("scrollDown").addClass("scrollUp"); 
		}
		c = currentScrollTop;
	});
      </script>

           <header>
            <h3 class="news-title area-primopiano" hp-img="/webimages/img_700/2021/3/21/655f3a7483a879aa55f939c33c687e36.jpg">
             <a href="/sito/notizie/sport/2021/03/19/serie-a-roma-napoli-formazioni_b9523dd1-aaef-46dd-8238-bcc818a747eb.html">

              <br/>
              Doppietta di Mertens
             </a>

             E' il posticipo serale della 28esima di Serie a
            </p>
           </div>
           <a class="img-photo" href="/sito/notizie/sport/2021/03/19/serie-a-roma-napoli-formazioni_b9523dd1-aaef-46dd-8238-bcc818a747eb.html" title="Soccer: Serie A; Roma vs Napoli">

         function millisecs(dateInString) {

}


advs = [];
i=0;
$(".ansacom-box").each(function(index) {
	pub = $(this).attr("data-pub");
	newsDate = new Date(pub);		
	time = (new Date()).getTime();
	from = (time - newsDate.getTime()) / 3600000;
	//console.log(parseInt(from)<=(24*counts[index]))
	if (counts[index]!=0 && parseInt(from)<=(24*counts[index])) { 
		advs[i] = index;
		i++;
	} 
	//console.log("from : " + from);
	//console.log(advs)
});

          <script>
           function insertHtml(id, html)

adv = unit_template.replace(/UNIT_ID/g, unit_id_300x100_top);
adv = adv.replace(/SLOT/g, slot_300x100_top);
console.log(slot_300x100_top);
$("#adv_300x100_top").append(adv);
}
          </script>
         </div>
         <!-- /316475115/ansa_desktop_hp_300x250_2 -->
         <div class="span4 adv-phone advr15 hidden-tablet" style="min-height:0px; width:300px; margin-top: 20px;">
          <div id="adv_300x250_bottom">
          </div>
          <script>
           function insertHtml(id, html)
{
var ele = document.getElementById(id);
ele.innerHTML = html;
var codes = ele.getElementsByTagName("script");
for(var i=0;i<codes.length;i++)
{
eval(codes[i].text);
}
}

var userAccept = $.cookie('cb-enabled');
//var cookieAccepted = (userAccept != null && userAccept.indexOf('accepted')!=-1);
var cookieAccepted = (userAccept != null);

if (cookieAccepted && !withinCMS() && !checkADV()) {
var unit_template = "<script>\
googletag.cmd.push(function() {\
googletag.defineSlot(\'SLOT\', [[300, 250]], \'UNIT_ID\').addService(googletag.pubads());\
googletag.pubads().enableLazyLoad();\
googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();\
googletag.pubads().collapseEmptyDivs();\
googletag.enableServices();\
});\
<\/script>\
<div id='UNIT_ID' style='height:250px; width:300px;'>\
<script>\
googletag.cmd.push(function() { googletag.display(\'UNIT_ID\'); });\
<\/script>\
</div>";

adv = unit_template.replace(/UNIT_ID/g, unit_id_300x250_bottom);
adv = adv.replace(/SLOT/g, slot_300x250_bottom);
console.log(slot_300x250_bottom);
$("#adv_300x250_bottom").append(adv);
}
          </script>
         </div>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    var	pageTitle = document.title;
	var	pageUrl = window.location.href;
	//Parameters for the Popup window
	var winWidth 	= 650;	
	var winHeight	= 450;
	var winLeft   	= ($(window).width()  - winWidth)  / 2;
	var winTop    	= ($(window).height() - winHeight) / 2;	
	var winOptions   = 'width='  + winWidth  + ',height=' + winHeight + ',top=' + winTop + ',left='   + winLeft;

	//user clicks on a share button
	$('.button-wrap').click(function(event) {
		
			var shareName = $(this).attr('class').split(' ')[0]; //get the first class name of clicked element

			switch (shareName) //switch to different links based on different social name
			{
				case 'facebook':
					var openLink = 'https://www.facebook.com/sharer/sharer.php?u=' + encodeURIComponent(pageUrl) + '&amp;title=' + encodeURIComponent(pageTitle);
					break;
				case 'twitter':
					//var openLink = 'http://twitter.com/home?status=' + encodeURIComponent(pageTitle + ' ' + pageUrl);
					var openLink = '//twitter.com/intent/tweet?text=' + encodeURIComponent(pageTitle + ' ' + pageUrl);
					break;
				case 'digg':
					var openLink = 'http://www.digg.com/submit?phase=2&amp;url=' + encodeURIComponent(pageUrl) + '&amp;title=' + encodeURIComponent(pageTitle);
					break;
				case 'stumbleupon':
					var openLink = 'http://www.stumbleupon.com/submit?url=' + encodeURIComponent(pageUrl) + '&amp;title=' + encodeURIComponent(pageTitle);
					break;
				case 'delicious':
					var openLink = 'http://del.icio.us/post?url=' + encodeURIComponent(pageUrl) + '&amp;title=' + encodeURIComponent(pageTitle);
					break;
				case 'google':
					var openLink = 'https://plus.google.com/share?url=' + encodeURIComponent(pageUrl) + '&amp;title=' + encodeURIComponent(pageTitle);
					break;
				case 'email':
					var openLink = 'mailto:?subject=' + pageTitle + '&body=Ti suggerisco questo link: ' + pageUrl;
					break;
				case 'linkedin':
					var openLink = 'http://www.linkedin.com/shareArticle?mini=true&url='+encodeURIComponent(pageUrl)+'&amp;title='+encodeURIComponent(pageTitle)+'&summary=&source=ansa.it';
					break;
				case 'pinterest':
					var openLink = 'http://pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url='+encodeURIComponent(pageUrl)+'&amp;description='+encodeURIComponent(pageTitle);
					break;
			}
				
		//open Popup window and redirect user to share website.
		window.open(openLink,'_blank',winOptions);
		$('#share-div').hide();
		return false;
	});
   </script>
